        <script type="text/javascript">
            function fnFilterColumn(i, txtVal) {
                $('#tbl_data').dataTable().fnFilter(txtVal, i, true, true);
            }

            $(document).ready(function() {
                $('#tbl_data').dataTable();
                reloadStylesheets();

                $('a.chFilter').click(function(event) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    if ($(this).text() == 'क्ष')
                        fnFilterColumn(2, '(^[क्ष])');
                    else if ($(this).text() == 'त्र')
                        fnFilterColumn(2, '(^[त्र])');
                    else if ($(this).text() == 'ज्ञ')
                        fnFilterColumn(2, '(^[ज्ञ])');
                    else if ($(this).text() != 'All')
                        fnFilterColumn(2, '(^[' + $(this).text() + '])');
                    else
                        fnFilterColumn(2, '');
                });

                $(document).on('click', 'button.btnData', function() {
                    $('#frmSubmit').append('<input type="hidden" name="hidData" value="' + $(this).attr('name') + '">');
                    $('#frmSubmit').appendTo($('body'));
                    $('#frmSubmit').submit();
                });
            });
